Fire WallCracker: Greetings from FOSSCell NITC.

We are excited to present the October edition of Friday Night FOSS, our monthly mini-hackathon dedicated to developing and exploring open source projects.

We are also excited to announce that the hackathon will feature a 2-hour workshop on 'Reclaim Protocol' conducted by a team of experts from Reclaim. If you're a developer, this is a good opportunity to build apps that import user data from other websites even when the websites do not provide APIs while valuing user security, privacy, and sovereignty. The Reclaim Protocol enables websites to apply digital signatures to the data they transmit, guaranteeing its legitimacy for users. It offers a decentralized version, where multiple attestors independently verify data authenticity, creating trust through economic incentives. You can learn more about the Reclaim Protocol here.

The workshop will be followed by a codesprint where you and your team of 4 members or less can work on any open-source project using the Reclaim protocol. Don't forget to add your bit of magic to the code as the best projects have a chance to receive grants from the Reclaim team. All participants will be provided refreshments to keep you energised throughout the event!

Join us on 20th October at 6:00pm to discover the exciting world of Reclaim. The venue will be announced soon.

Given the limited seating capacity, we prioritize participants with frontend/backend development background to ensure an effective and productive workshop experience. Selected students will receive a confirmation mail from our team by 17th October.

Interested students may register for the event by filling out the Opnform here.
https://opnform.com/forms/friday-night-foss-v2-reclaim-edition-registraion-rexi2r

Regards,
Secretary
Free and Open Source Software Cell
NIT Calicut
https://fosscell.org

Pratheek: def factorial(n):
    if 0 <= n < 2:
        return 1
    return n*factorial(n-1)

print(factorial(5))
Pratheek: def fib(n):
    if n==0:
        return 0
    elif 0 < n < 3:
        return 1
    return fib(n) + fib(n-1)

    if n==0:
        return 0
    elif 0 < n < 3:
        return 1
    return fib(n-1) + fib(n-2)
print(fib(8))

Fire WallCracker: #include<stdio.h>
int n;
int M[100];
int G[100];
char markstograde(int marks);
int gradecount( char grade);
int main()
{
    printf("enter the value of n(n>=5 && n<=100):");
    scanf("%d",&n);
    if(n<5 || n>100){
        printf("invalid data");
        return 1;}
   printf("Enter the marks of each student:\n") ;
   for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        scanf("%d",&M[i]);
        G[i]=markstograde(M[i]);
    }
    printgradecount();
    return 0;
}
char markstograde(int marks){
        if(marks>=80 && marks<=100)
        return 'A';
         if(marks>=60 && marks<=79)
        return 'B';
         if(marks>=50 && marks<=59)
        return 'P';
         if(marks>=0 && marks<=49)
        return 'F';
        return 'X';
    }
int gradecount( char grade){
    int count=0;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if(G[i]==grade){
            count++; }
    }
    return count;
}
void printgradecount(void){
    char grade[]={'A','B','P','F'};
    printf("grade\tcount\n");
    for(int i=0;i<4;i++){
    int count=gradecount(grade[i]);
    printf("%c\t\t%d\n",grade[i],count);
    }
}
Fire WallCracker: #include<stdio.h>
int findHighestmark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID);
int findLowestmark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID);
float calculateAveragemark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID);
float calculateTotalmark( int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID);
int main()
{
    int n,i,j;
    printf("Enter the value of n(n>=5 || n<=100):");
    scanf("%d",&n);
    if(n<5 && n>100){
        printf("invalid data");
        return 1;}
    int Marks[n][3];
    for(i=0;i<n;i++){
        for(j=0;j<=2;j++){
            scanf("%d",&Marks[i][j]); }
    }
    for(i=0;i<n;i++){
        for(j=0;j<=2;j++){
            printf("%d\t",Marks[i][j]);}
            printf("\n");
    }
   int choice;
   do{
       printf("\nPlease enter a number indicating your choice\n");
       printf("1: highest mark in a course\n");
       printf(" 2: lowest mark in a course\n");
       printf(" 3: average marks for a course\n");
       printf(" 4: total marks of a student\n");
       printf(" 0: exit\n");
    scanf("%d",&choice);
    switch(choice){
        case 1:printf("Enter courseID:");
               int courseID;
               scanf("%d",&courseID);
               if(courseID>=0 || courseID<3){
                   int Highestmark=findHighestmark(Marks,n,courseID);
                   printf("Highest mark in course %d=%d",courseID,Highestmark);
               }
               else printf("invalid data");
               break;
        case 2:printf("Enter courseID:");
               scanf("%d",&courseID);
               if(courseID>=0 || courseID<3){
                   int Lowestmark=findLowestmark(Marks,n,courseID);
                   printf("Lowest mark in course %d=%d",courseID,Lowestmark);
               }
               else printf("invalid data"); 
               break;
        case 3:printf("Enter courseID:");
               scanf("%d",&courseID);
               if(courseID>=0 || courseID<3){
                  float Averagemark=calculateAveragemark(Marks,n,courseID);
                   printf("Average mark in course %d=%f",courseID,Averagemark);
               }
               else printf("invalid data");
               break;
        case 4:printf("Enter StudentID:");
               int StudentID;
               scanf("%d",&StudentID);
               if(StudentID>=0 || StudentID<n){
                  float Totalmark=calculateTotalmark(Marks,n,StudentID);
                   printf("Total marks of student %d=%f",StudentID,Totalmark);
               }
               else printf("invalid data");
               break;
        case 0:printf("exiting the programme");
               break;
       default:printf("invalid choice");
    }
    }while(choice!=0);
    
    return 0;
    
}
int findHighestmark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID){
    int max=Marks[0][courseID];
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
    if(Marks[i][courseID]>max){
        max=Marks[i][courseID];
    }
}
return max;
}
int findLowestmark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID){
    int min=Marks[0][courseID];
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++){
    if(Marks[i][courseID]<min){
        min=Marks[i][courseID];
    }
}
return min;
}
float calculateAveragemark(int Marks[][3],int n,int courseID){
    float sum=0;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
        sum+=Marks[i][courseID];
    }
    return sum/n;
}
float calculateTotalmark(int Marks[][3],int n,int StudentID){
    int totalmarks=0;
    for(int j=0;j<3;j++){
        totalmarks+=Marks[StudentID][j];
    }
    return totalmarks;
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#define pos_t int


class Node {
    public:
    int data;
    Node *next;

    Node(int data) {
        this -> data = data;
    }
};

class SinglyLinkedList {
    Node *link;
    public:
    Node *head;
    SinglyLinkedList() {
        this->head = nullptr;
    }
    void add_node(int data) {
        Node *new_node = new Node(data);
        if (this->head == nullptr) {
            new_node->next = this->head;
            this->head = new_node;
            this->link = new_node;
        }
        else {
            link->next = new_node;
            new_node->next = nullptr;
            link = new_node;
        }
    }
    void insert_node(int data, pos_t position) {
        Node *new_node = new Node(data);
        if (position > 1){
        Node *ptr = head;
        for(pos_t i = 2; i < position; i++) {
            ptr = ptr->next;
        }
        new_node->next = ptr->next;
        ptr->next = new_node;
        }
        else {
            new_node->next = head;
            head = new_node;
        }
    }
};

int main() {
    SinglyLinkedList s;
    s.add_node(5);
    s.add_node(10);
    s.add_node(15);
    s.add_node(20);
    Node *ptr = s.head;
    while(ptr != nullptr) {
        std::cout << ptr->data << std::endl;
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    s.insert_node(25, 3);
    std::cout << "============================" << std::endl;
    ptr = s.head;
    while(ptr != nullptr) {
        std::cout << ptr->data << std::endl;
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    return 0;
}
Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#define pos_t int

class Node {
    public:
    int data;
    Node *next;
    Node *prev;

    Node(int data) {
        this -> data = data;
    }
};

class DoublyLinkedList {
    Node *link;
    public:
    Node *head;
    DoublyLinkedList() {
        this->head = nullptr;
    }
    void add_node(int data) {
        Node *new_node = new Node(data);
        if (this->head == nullptr) {
            new_node->next = this->head;
            new_node->prev = nullptr;
            this->head = new_node;
            this->link = new_node;
        }
        else {
            link->next = new_node;
            new_node->next = nullptr;
            new_node->prev = link;
            link = new_node;
        }
    }
    void insert_node(int data, pos_t position) {
        Node *new_node = new Node(data);
        if (position > 1){
        Node *ptr = head;
        for(pos_t i = 2; i < position; i++) {
            ptr = ptr->next;
        }
        new_node->next = ptr->next;
        new_node->prev = ptr;
        ptr->next = new_node;
        (new_node->next)->prev = new_node;
        }
        else {
            new_node->next = head;
            new_node->prev = head->prev;
            head->prev = new_node;
            head = new_node;
        }
    }
};

void fwd(DoublyLinkedList, Node **);
void bwd(DoublyLinkedList, Node **);

int main() {
    DoublyLinkedList s;
    s.add_node(5);
    s.add_node(10);
    s.add_node(15);
    s.add_node(20);
    Node *ptr = s.head;
    fwd(s, &ptr);
    std::cout << "========================" << std::endl;
    bwd(s, &ptr);
    std::cout << "========================" << std::endl;
    s.insert_node(25, 3);
    fwd(s, &ptr);
    std::cout << "========================" << std::endl;
    bwd(s, &ptr);
    return 0;
}

void fwd(DoublyLinkedList s, Node **ptr) {
    while(true) {
        std::cout << (*ptr)->data << std::endl;
        if((*ptr)->next == nullptr) {
            break;
        }
        else {
            *ptr = (*ptr)->next;
        }
    }
}

void bwd(DoublyLinkedList s, Node **ptr) {
    while(true) {
        std::cout << (*ptr)->data << std::endl;
        if ((*ptr)->prev == nullptr) {
            break;
        }
        else {
            *ptr = (*ptr)->prev;
        }
    }
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>

void mergeSort(std::vector<int>& , int, int);
void merge(std::vector<int>&, int, int, int);

int main() {
    std::vector<int> vec {2, 5, 9, 8, 6, 1, 3};
    mergeSort(vec, 0, vec.size() - 1);
    for(auto x: vec) {
        std::cout << x << " ";
    }
    return 0;
}

void mergeSort(std::vector<int>& vec, int low, int high) {
    if (low < high) {
        int mid = (low + high)/2;
        mergeSort(vec, low, mid);
        mergeSort(vec, mid + 1, high);
        merge(vec, low, mid, high);
    }
    else{}
}

void merge(std::vector<int>& vec, int low, int mid, int high) {
    int *ptr1 = &vec[low];
    int *ptr2 = &vec[mid + 1];
    std::vector<int> newVec;
    while(ptr1 <= &vec[mid] && ptr2 <= &vec[high]) {
        if(*ptr1 <= *ptr2) {
            newVec.emplace_back(*ptr1);
            ptr1++;
        }
        else {
            newVec.emplace_back(*ptr2);
            ptr2++;
        }
    }
    if(ptr1 != &vec[mid]){
        for(ptr1; ptr1 <= &vec[mid]; ptr1++) {
            newVec.emplace_back(*ptr1);
        }
    }
    else if (ptr2 != &vec[high]) {
        for(ptr2; ptr2 < &vec[high]; ptr2++) {
            newVec.emplace_back(*ptr2);
            ptr2++;
        }
    }
    else return;
    for (int i = low; i <= high; i++) {
        vec[i] = newVec[i - low];
    }
    return;
}

Fire WallCracker: To clear credentials stored in Git Credential Manager, you can follow these steps depending on your operating system:

Windows
Open Credential Manager:

Press Win + S, type Credential Manager, and open it.
Find Git Credentials:

Go to the Windows Credentials tab.
Look for entries related to git, such as git:https://[repository URL].
Remove the Credentials:

Click on the entry and then click Remove.
Test the Result:

The next time you push or pull, Git will prompt for your username and password.

Fire WallCracker: To robustly hide a user account like harsa from GDM and general visibility â€” while still keeping it fully functional (e.g., sudo access, login via TTY or "Not Listed") â€” you want to use a combination of secure and reversible techniques.

Here's a robust, production-safe method for hiding the harsa account:


---

âœ… Step-by-Step: Robustly Hide harsa from GDM & GUI

âœ… 1. Create the user (if not already done)

sudo adduser harsa
sudo usermod -aG sudo harsa


---

âœ… 2. Mark harsa as a system account in AccountsService

This makes GDM and other GUI tools ignore it.

Create file:

sudo mkdir -p /var/lib/AccountsService/users/
sudo nano /var/lib/AccountsService/users/harsa

Add contents:

[User]
SystemAccount=true

Save and close.

Restart AccountsService:

sudo systemctl restart accounts-daemon


---

âœ… 3. Use GDM's custom.conf to double-confirm exclusion

sudo nano /etc/gdm3/custom.conf

Add under [daemon]:

[daemon]
Exclude=harsa

If there are already other users listed, do:

Exclude=student,harsa

Then restart GDM:

sudo systemctl restart gdm3


---

âœ… 4. (Optional) Change UID to system range (e.g., <1000)

Linux considers UIDs below 1000 as system accounts â€” hidden by default.

âš ï¸ Caution: This can break file permissions if done carelessly.

sudo usermod -u 998 harsa
sudo groupmod -g 998 harsa

Then fix file ownership:

sudo find / -user 1001 -exec chown -h harsa {} \;
sudo find / -group 1001 -exec chgrp -h harsa {} \;

(Replace 1001 with the original UID/GID of harsa)


---

âœ… 5. Hide Home Directory (Optional for stealth)

You can move the home directory to a hidden location:

sudo mv /home/harsa /var/hidden-harsa
sudo usermod -d /var/hidden-harsa harsa

Make sure itâ€™s owned correctly:

sudo chown -R harsa:harsa /var/hidden-harsa


---

ğŸ” Final Result

Feature	Status

Appears in GDM login screen	âŒ Hidden
Can use "Not listed?"	âœ… Yes
Can login via TTY	âœ… Yes (Ctrl+Alt+F2, etc.)
Has sudo rights	âœ… Yes
Obvious home folder	âŒ Hidden (/var/hidden-harsa)

      mkdir -p $out/bin $out/share/java
      cp $src $out/share/java/tlauncher.jar

        --add-flags "java" \
        --add-flags "-jar" \
        --add-flags "$out/share/java/tlauncher.jar"
    '';
  };

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

class SegmentTree {
private:
    vector<long long> tree;
    vector<long long> lazy_add;
    vector<long long> lazy_set;
    vector<bool> has_set;
    int n;

    void build(vector<int>& arr, int node, int start, int end) {
        if (start == end) {
            tree[node] = arr[start];
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            build(arr, 2 * node + 1, start, mid);
            build(arr, 2 * node + 2, mid + 1, end);
            tree[node] = tree[2 * node + 1] + tree[2 * node + 2];
        }
    }

    void push_down(int node, int start, int end) {
        if (has_set[node]) {
            tree[node] = lazy_set[node] * (end - start + 1);
            if (start != end) {
                lazy_set[2 * node + 1] = lazy_set[node];
                lazy_set[2 * node + 2] = lazy_set[node];
                lazy_add[2 * node + 1] = 0;
                lazy_add[2 * node + 2] = 0;
                has_set[2 * node + 1] = true;
                has_set[2 * node + 2] = true;
            }
            lazy_set[node] = 0;
            has_set[node] = false;
        }
        
        if (lazy_add[node] != 0) {
            tree[node] += lazy_add[node] * (end - start + 1);
            if (start != end) {
                lazy_add[2 * node + 1] += lazy_add[node];
                lazy_add[2 * node + 2] += lazy_add[node];
            }
            lazy_add[node] = 0;
        }
    }

    void range_add(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r, long long val) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        if (r < start || end < l) return;
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            lazy_add[node] += val;
            push_down(node, start, end);
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            range_add(2 * node + 1, start, mid, l, r, val);
            range_add(2 * node + 2, mid + 1, end, l, r, val);
            tree[node] = tree[2 * node + 1] + tree[2 * node + 2];
        }
    }

    void range_set(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r, long long val) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        if (r < start || end < l) return;
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            lazy_set[node] = val;
            lazy_add[node] = 0;
            has_set[node] = true;
            push_down(node, start, end);
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            range_set(2 * node + 1, start, mid, l, r, val);
            range_set(2 * node + 2, mid + 1, end, l, r, val);
            tree[node] = tree[2 * node + 1] + tree[2 * node + 2];
        }
    }

    long long range_sum(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        if (r < start || end < l) return 0;
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            return tree[node];
        }
        int mid = (start + end) / 2;
        long long left_sum = range_sum(2 * node + 1, start, mid, l, r);
        long long right_sum = range_sum(2 * node + 2, mid + 1, end, l, r);
        return left_sum + right_sum;
    }

    void get_final_values(int node, int start, int end, vector<long long>& result) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        if (start == end) {
            result[start] = tree[node];
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            get_final_values(2 * node + 1, start, mid, result);
            get_final_values(2 * node + 2, mid + 1, end, result);
        }
    }

public:
    SegmentTree(vector<int>& arr) {
        n = arr.size();
        tree.resize(4 * n, 0);
        lazy_add.resize(4 * n, 0);
        lazy_set.resize(4 * n, 0);
        has_set.resize(4 * n, false);
        build(arr, 0, 0, n - 1);
    }

    void add(int l, int r, long long val) {
        range_add(0, 0, n - 1, l, r, val);
    }

    void subtract(int l, int r, long long val) {
        range_add(0, 0, n - 1, l, r, -val);
    }

    void set(int l, int r, long long val) {
        range_set(0, 0, n - 1, l, r, val);
    }

    void special_operation(int l, int r) {
        long long sum_val = range_sum(0, 0, n - 1, l, r);
        range_add(0, 0, n - 1, l, r, sum_val);
    }

    vector<long long> get_final_list() {
        vector<long long> result(n);
        get_final_values(0, 0, n - 1, result);
        return result;
    }
};

int main() {
    int N, P;
    cin >> N >> P;
    
    vector<int> initial_list(N);
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cin >> initial_list[i];
    }
    
    SegmentTree seg_tree(initial_list);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < P; i++) {
        int op, X, Y;
        long long V;
        cin >> op >> X >> Y >> V;
        
        // Convert to 0-based indexing
        X--;
        Y--;
        
        switch (op) {
            case 1:
                seg_tree.add(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 2:
                seg_tree.subtract(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 3:
                seg_tree.set(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 4:
                seg_tree.special_operation(X, Y);
                break;
        }
    }
    
    vector<long long> final_list = seg_tree.get_final_list();
    
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cout << final_list[i];
        if (i < N - 1) {
            cout << " ";
        }
    }
    cout << endl;
    
    return 0;
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int N, P;
    cin >> N >> P;
    
    vector<long long> arr(N);
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cin >> arr[i];
    }
    
    for (int i = 0; i < P; i++) {
        int op, X, Y;
        long long V;
        cin >> op >> X >> Y >> V;
        X--; Y--;
        
        if (op == 1) {
            for (int j = X; j <= Y; j++) arr[j] += V;
        }
        else if (op == 2) {
            for (int j = X; j <= Y; j++) arr[j] -= V;
        }
        else if (op == 3) {
            for (int j = X; j <= Y; j++) arr[j] = V;
        }
        else if (op == 4) {
            long long sum = 0;
            for (int j = X; j <= Y; j++) sum += arr[j];
            for (int j = X; j <= Y; j++) arr[j] += sum;
        }
    }
    
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cout << arr[i] << " ";
    }
    
    return 0;
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

struct Node {
    long long sum;
    long long add;
    long long set;
    bool has_set;
    
    Node() : sum(0), add(0), set(0), has_set(false) {}
};

class SegmentTree {
private:
    vector<Node> tree;
    int n;
    
    void build(vector<int>& arr, int node, int start, int end) {
        if (start == end) {
            tree[node].sum = arr[start];
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            build(arr, 2 * node, start, mid);
            build(arr, 2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end);
            tree[node].sum = tree[2 * node].sum + tree[2 * node + 1].sum;
        }
    }
    
    void push_down(int node, int start, int end) {
        if (tree[node].has_set) {
            long long set_val = tree[node].set;
            tree[node].sum = set_val * (end - start + 1);
            
            if (start != end) {
                tree[2 * node].set = set_val;
                tree[2 * node].has_set = true;
                tree[2 * node].add = 0;
                
                tree[2 * node + 1].set = set_val;
                tree[2 * node + 1].has_set = true;
                tree[2 * node + 1].add = 0;
            }
            
            tree[node].has_set = false;
            tree[node].set = 0;
        }
        
        if (tree[node].add != 0) {
            tree[node].sum += tree[node].add * (end - start + 1);
            
            if (start != end) {
                tree[2 * node].add += tree[node].add;
                tree[2 * node + 1].add += tree[node].add;
            }
            
            tree[node].add = 0;
        }
    }
    
    void update_add(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r, long long val) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        
        if (r < start || end < l) return;
        
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            tree[node].add += val;
            push_down(node, start, end);
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            update_add(2 * node, start, mid, l, r, val);
            update_add(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, l, r, val);
            tree[node].sum = tree[2 * node].sum + tree[2 * node + 1].sum;
        }
    }
    
    void update_set(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r, long long val) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        
        if (r < start || end < l) return;
        
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            tree[node].set = val;
            tree[node].has_set = true;
            tree[node].add = 0;
            push_down(node, start, end);
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            update_set(2 * node, start, mid, l, r, val);
            update_set(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, l, r, val);
            tree[node].sum = tree[2 * node].sum + tree[2 * node + 1].sum;
        }
    }
    
    long long query_sum(int node, int start, int end, int l, int r) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        
        if (r < start || end < l) return 0;
        
        if (l <= start && end <= r) {
            return tree[node].sum;
        }
        
        int mid = (start + end) / 2;
        long long left_sum = query_sum(2 * node, start, mid, l, r);
        long long right_sum = query_sum(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, l, r);
        return left_sum + right_sum;
    }
    
    void get_values(int node, int start, int end, vector<long long>& result) {
        push_down(node, start, end);
        
        if (start == end) {
            result[start] = tree[node].sum;
        } else {
            int mid = (start + end) / 2;
            get_values(2 * node, start, mid, result);
            get_values(2 * node + 1, mid + 1, end, result);
        }
    }

public:
    SegmentTree(vector<int>& arr) {
        n = arr.size();
        tree.resize(4 * n);
        build(arr, 1, 0, n - 1);
    }
    
    void add(int l, int r, long long val) {
        update_add(1, 0, n - 1, l, r, val);
    }
    
    void subtract(int l, int r, long long val) {
        update_add(1, 0, n - 1, l, r, -val);
    }
    
    void set(int l, int r, long long val) {
        update_set(1, 0, n - 1, l, r, val);
    }
    
    void special_operation(int l, int r) {
        long long sum_val = query_sum(1, 0, n - 1, l, r);
        update_add(1, 0, n - 1, l, r, sum_val);
    }
    
    vector<long long> get_final_list() {
        vector<long long> result(n);
        get_values(1, 0, n - 1, result);
        return result;
    }
};

int main() {
    int N, P;
    cin >> N >> P;
    
    vector<int> initial_list(N);
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cin >> initial_list[i];
    }
    
    SegmentTree seg_tree(initial_list);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < P; i++) {
        int op, X, Y;
        long long V;
        cin >> op >> X >> Y >> V;
        
        // Convert to 0-based indexing
        X--;
        Y--;
        
        switch (op) {
            case 1:
                seg_tree.add(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 2:
                seg_tree.subtract(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 3:
                seg_tree.set(X, Y, V);
                break;
            case 4:
                seg_tree.special_operation(X, Y);
                break;
        }
    }
    
    vector<long long> final_list = seg_tree.get_final_list();
    
    for (int i = 0; i < N; i++) {
        cout << final_list[i];
        if (i < N - 1) {
            cout << " ";
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

void dfs(int u, int parent, const vector<vector<int>>& graph, const vector<int>& efficiency, vector<vector<long long>>& dp) {
    dp[u][1] = efficiency[u];
    dp[u][0] = 0;

    for (int v : graph[u]) {
        if (v == parent) continue;
        dfs(v, u, graph, efficiency, dp);
        dp[u][1] += dp[v][0];
        dp[u][0] += max(dp[v][0], dp[v][1]);
    }
}

void maxEfficiency(vector<int> efficiency, vector<vector<int>> courtMemberYes) {
    int n = efficiency.size();
    vector<vector<int>> graph(n);

    for (const auto& edge : courtMemberYes) {
        int a = edge[0], b = edge[1];
        // Assuming 0-based indexing
        graph[a].push_back(b);
        graph[b].push_back(a);
    }

    vector<vector<long long>> dp(n, vector<long long>(2, 0));
    dfs(0, -1, graph, efficiency, dp);

    cout << max(dp[0][0], dp[0][1]) << endl;
}
Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<long long> A(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> A[i];
    }

    long long ans = 0;

    // Precompute products for each sum s = u+v
    vector<vector<long long>> sumProd(2 * n - 1);
    for (int s = 0; s <= 2 * n - 2; s++) {
        int start = max(0, s - (n - 1));
        int end = min(n - 1, s);
        int len = end - start + 1;
        sumProd[s].resize(len + 1, 0);
        for (int u = start; u <= end; u++) {
            int v = s - u;
            if (v >= 0 && v < n) {
                sumProd[s][u - start + 1] = sumProd[s][u - start] + A[u] * A[v];
            }
        }
    }

    // Try all k, i, j
    for (int k = 1; k <= n / 2; k++) {
        for (int i = 0; i <= n - k; i++) {
            for (int j = i + k; j <= n - k; j++) {
                int s = i + j + k - 1;
                int start_u = i;
                int end_u = i + k - 1;
                int base = max(0, s - (n - 1));
                long long total = sumProd[s][end_u - base + 1] - sumProd[s][start_u - base];
                ans = max(ans, total);
            }
        }
    }

    cout << max(0LL, ans) << endl;
    return 0;
}

void dfs(int u, int parent, const vector<vector<int> >& graph, const vector<int>& efficiency, vector<vector<long long> >& dp) {
    dp[u][1] = efficiency[u];
    dp[u][0] = 0;

void maxEfficiency(vector<int> efficiency, vector<vector<int> > courtMemberYes) {
    int n = efficiency.size();
    vector<vector<int> > graph(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < courtMemberYes.size(); i++) {
        int a = courtMemberYes[i][0];
        int b = courtMemberYes[i][1];
        // Adjust for 0-based indexing if input is 1-based
        // If input is 0-based, use as is
        graph[a].push_back(b);
        graph[b].push_back(a);
    }

    vector<vector<long long> > dp(n, vector<long long>(2, 0));
    dfs(0, -1, graph, efficiency, dp);

    cout << max(dp[0][0], dp[0][1]) << endl;
}

    int n;

    vector<int> efficiency(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> efficiency[i];
    }
    int x, y;
    cin >> x >> y;

    for (int i = 0; i < x; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < y; j++) {
            cin >> edges[i][j];
        }
    }

    maxEfficiency(efficiency, edges);
    return 0;
}

        dfs(v, u, graph, efficiency, dp);

    int n = efficiency.size();

    // OLD: for (const auto& edge : courtMemberYes) {
    // NEW: Replace range-based loop with index-based loop
    for (int i = 0; i < courtMemberYes.size(); i++) {
        // OLD: int a = edge[0], b = edge[1];
        // NEW: Access elements directly
        int a = courtMemberYes[i][0];
        int b = courtMemberYes[i][1];
        graph[a].push_back(b);
        graph[b].push_back(a);

    vector<vector<long long>> dp(n, vector<long long>(2, 0));
    dfs(0, -1, graph, efficiency, dp);

    cout << max(dp[0][0], dp[0][1]) << endl;
}

void maxEfficiency(vector<int> efficiency, vector<vector<int> > courtMemberYes) {
    int n = efficiency.size();
    vector<vector<int> > graph(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < courtMemberYes.size(); i++) {

        int b = courtMemberYes[i][1] - 1;
        graph[a].push_back(b);
        graph[b].push_back(a);

    vector<vector<long long> > dp(n, vector<long long>(2, 0));

    cout << max(dp[0][0], dp[0][1]) << endl;

void dfs(int u, int parent, const vector<vector<int> >& graph, const vector<int>& efficiency, vector<vector<long long> >& dp) {
    dp[u][1] = efficiency[u];
    dp[u][0] = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < graph[u].size(); i++) {
        int v = graph[u][i];
        if (v == parent) continue;
        dfs(v, u, graph, efficiency, dp);
        dp[u][1] += dp[v][0];
        dp[u][0] += max(dp[v][0], dp[v][1]);
    }
}

void maxEfficiency(vector<int> efficiency, vector<vector<int> > edges) {
    int n = efficiency.size();
    vector<vector<int> > graph(n);

    for (int i = 0; i < edges.size(); i++) {
        int a = edges[i][0] - 1;  // Convert to 0-based
        int b = edges[i][1] - 1;  // Convert to 0-based
        graph[a].push_back(b);
        graph[b].push_back(a);
    }

    vector<vector<long long> > dp(n, vector<long long>(2, 0));
    dfs(0, -1, graph, efficiency, dp);

    cout << max(dp[0][0], dp[0][1]) << endl;
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<int> efficiency(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> efficiency[i];
    }
    
    int m;  // number of edges
    cin >> m;
    vector<vector<int> > edges(m, vector<int>(2));
    
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        cin >> edges[i][0] >> edges[i][1];
    }

    maxEfficiency(efficiency, edges);
    return 0;
}

Fire WallCracker: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<long long> A(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        cin >> A[i];
    }

    long long ans = 0;

    // Precompute all products A[i] * A[j]
    vector<vector<long long>> product(n, vector<long long>(n, 0));
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            product[i][j] = A[i] * A[j];
        }
    }

    // Precompute prefix sums for each diagonal (i+j = constant)
    vector<vector<long long>> diagPrefix(2 * n);
    for (int s = 0; s < 2 * n; s++) {
        int start_i = max(0, s - (n - 1));
        int end_i = min(n - 1, s);
        int len = end_i - start_i + 1;
        if (len > 0) {
            diagPrefix[s].resize(len + 1, 0);
            for (int idx = 0; idx < len; idx++) {
                int i = start_i + idx;
                int j = s - i;
                diagPrefix[s][idx + 1] = diagPrefix[s][idx] + product[i][j];
            }
        }
    }

    // Find maximum sum for valid (i, j, k) combinations
    for (int k = 1; k <= n / 2; k++) {
        for (int i = 0; i <= n - k; i++) {
            // Instead of iterating over all j, we can optimize
            for (int j = i + k; j <= n - k; j++) {
                int diag = i + j + k - 1;
                if (diag < diagPrefix.size() && !diagPrefix[diag].empty()) {
                    int start_idx = i;
                    int end_idx = i + k - 1;
                    int base = max(0, diag - (n - 1));
                    
                    if (start_idx - base >= 0 && end_idx - base + 1 < diagPrefix[diag].size()) {
                        long long sum = diagPrefix[diag][end_idx - base + 1] - diagPrefix[diag][start_idx - base];
                        ans = max(ans, sum);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    cout << ans << endl;
    return 0;
}
